# ::id dip_test_0001.1
# ::snt ITALY send that Hey Austria! I know AT is one of the least successful alliances in the game, so I'm super down to work together here, especially if we can get Russia and Turkey fighting.
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Italy"))
      :ARG1 (a / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a2 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Austria")))
            :ARG3 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Russia"))
                  :op2 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Turkey"))))
      :ARG3 c2)
DAIDE: PRP (ALY (ITA AUS) VSS (RUS TUR))

# ::id dip_test_0001.2
# ::snt FRANCE send that Hey Germany! Just reaching out to say I think our two nations tend to benefit a ton from working together, and I'm very down to work together if you'd be interested!
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (a / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a2 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "England"))))
      :ARG3 (c3 / country
            :name (n3 / name
                  :op1 "Germany")))
PARA-DAIDE: PRP (ALY (FRA ENG))

# ::id dip_test_0001.3
# ::snt FRANCE send that Hey Italy! I think our two nations tend to do best when we can leave each other alone, so I'd love it if we could agree to not harass one another?
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (a / attack-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG0 (a2 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "England")))
            :ARG1 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Italy")))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP (attack-01 :polarity "-" :ARG0 AND FRA ENG :ARG1 ITA)

# ::id dip_test_0001.4
# ::snt GERMANY send that Hey France, absolutely! Are you up for a DMZ in Burgundy?
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Germany"))
      :ARG1 (a / and
            :op1 (w / warn-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "England"))
                  :ARG1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "France"))
                  :ARG2 c)
            :op2 (d / demilitarize-01
                  :op1 c2
                  :op2 c3)
            :ARG1-of d
            :ARG2 (p2 / province
                  :name (n4 / name
                        :op1 "Burgundy")))
      :ARG3 c3
      :polarity (a2 / amr-unknown))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP (AND (warn-01 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 FRA :ARG2 GER) (demilitarize-01 :op1 ENG :op2 FRA))

# ::id dip_test_0001.5
# ::snt TURKEY send that Hey Russia, just wanna say good luck and hopefully we can be friends!
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Italy"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Russia"))))
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 ITA :ARG1 ALY (ITA RUS) :ARG2 RUS))

# ::id dip_test_0001.19
# ::snt ENGLAND send that Hey Russia! I'd like to take Norway this year, but I'm not planning on sending any further units your way. If there's anything I can do to help you, feel free to ask!
AMR:

      :ARG0 (c / country

                  :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name

                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (p2 / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Norway"))
                  :time (d / date-entity
                        :year 1902))
            :ARG2 (c3 / country
                  :name (n4 / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 SCD (ENG NWY) :ARG2 GER))

# ::id dip_test_0001.26
# ::snt FRANCE send that Excellent! I feel the same way, so I look forward to our alliance! Would you be alright with a DMZ in Pie, Gol, and W Med?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (a2 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c / country
                        :name (n / name
                              :op1 "France"))
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "England"))))
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (d / demilitarize-01
                  :ARG1 (a4 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG2 (a5 / and
                        :op1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Piedmont"))
                        :op2 (p3 / province
                              :name (n4 / name
                                    :op1 "Greece"))
                        :op3 (p4 / province
                              :name (n5 / name
                                    :op1 "Giles"))))
            :ARG3 c2))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (ALY (FRA ENG)) (PRP (DMZ (FRA ENG) (PIE GRE (province :name (name :op1 "Giles")))))

# ::id dip_test_0001.29
# ::snt TURKEY send that I'm gonna move for Bulgaria for now. Are you moving for Austria?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Italy"))
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (u / unit
                        :mod c)
                  :ARG2 (p / province
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Bulgaria")))
            :ARG2 (c2 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Austria")))
      :op2 (m2 / move-01
            :ARG1 (u2 / unit
                  :mod c)
            :ARG2 (c3 / country
                  :name (n4 / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))
            :polarity (a2 / amr-unknown)))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (tell-01 :ARG0 ITA :ARG1 (unit :mod ITA) MTO BUL :ARG2 AUS) ((unit :mod ITA) MTO GER)

      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP ((tell-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG1 (propose-01 :ARG0 RUS :ARG3 ITA) :ARG2 ITA))

# ::id dip_test_0001.31
# ::snt ENGLAND send that I don't think I can do that; it would leave me completely open to France. However, I am planning on taking it with a fleet.
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (p / possible-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG1 (h / have-03
                  :ARG0 (c / country
                        :name (n / name
                              :op1 "England"))
                  :ARG1 (p2 / province
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Denmark"))))
      :op2 (p3 / possible-01
            :ARG1 (h2 / have-03
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 p2
                  :instrument (f / fleet))))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (possible-01 :polarity "-" :ARG1 (have-03 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 DEN)) (possible-01 :ARG1 (have-03 :ARG0 ENG :ARG1 DEN :instrument (fleet)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.32
# ::snt RUSSIA send that Hey Austria, sounds good to me! Bounce Galicia and work together sounds good to me, I think the R/A is one of the more powerful alliances on the board.
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))
            :ARG1 (b / bounce-03
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 (u / unit
                              :mod c)
                        :op2 (u2 / unit
                              :mod (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "Austria"))))
                  :ARG3 (p2 / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Galicia")))
            :ARG3 c2)
      :op2 (a3 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a4 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :op2 c)))
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (PRP ((bounce-03 :ARG1 AND (unit :mod RUS) (unit :mod AUS) :ARG3 GAL))) (ALY (ITA RUS))

# ::id dip_test_0001.33
# ::snt ITALY send that I'd be super down for that. I don't see any point in either of us moving there, and it just ties up a unit for each of us that we can use elsewhere.
AMR:
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Italy"))
      :ARG1 (m / move-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG1 (o / or
                  :op1 (u / unit
                        :mod c)
                  :op2 (u2 / unit
                        :mod (c2 / country
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany"))))
            :ARG2 (p2 / province
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Tyrolia")))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP (XDO (NOT ((or :op1 (unit :mod ITA) :op2 (unit :mod GER)) MTO TYR)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.35
# ::snt ENGLAND send that I have. He wants me to not take Norway with an army. Which is fine by me but I'm not going to oblige. What do you think of him?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (h / have-03
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Germany"))
                  :ARG1 (p2 / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Norway")))
            :ARG3 c2)
      :op2 (a2 / agree-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (h2 / have-03
                  :polarity -
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 p2)
            :ARG2 c))
DAIDE: AND (PRP (SCD (GER NWY))) (NOT (YES (PRP (NOT (SCD (ENG NWY))))))

# ::id dip_test_0001.36

                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Fairway")))
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.38
# ::snt ENGLAND send that Let's do an E/F against Germany. I'd like a second build this year, though. Do you mind supporting me into Belgium?
AMR:
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / and
                  :op1 (a3 / attack-01
                        :ARG0 (a4 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "France")))
                        :ARG1 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany")))
                  :op2 a3
                  :ARG0 (a5 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG1 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Germany"))
                  :time (d / date-entity
                        :year 1905)))
      :ARG3 c2
      :op2 p
      :ARG0 c2
      :ARG1 (s / support-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (u / unit
                        :mod c2)
                  :ARG2 (p2 / province
                        :name (n5 / name
                              :op1 "Belgium"))))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: AND (PRP (AND (attack-01 :ARG0 AND ENG FRA :ARG1 GER) (attack-01 :ARG0 AND ENG FRA :ARG1 GER))) (PRP (AND (attack-01 :ARG0 AND ENG FRA :ARG1 GER) (attack-01 :ARG0 AND ENG FRA :ARG1 GER)))

                                    :op1 "Picardy")))))
      :ARG3 c2)
PARTIAL-DAIDE: PRP (AND (GER SUP (unit :mod FRA) MTO BEL) (FRA SUP (unit :mod GER) MTO BEL))

# ::id dip_test_0001.844
# ::snt GERMANY send that That would give England Holland, so they'd get a build, and probably make a fleet in Liverpool to stop you from taking it. If you go from Burgundy, you get a build, you are guaranteed to take Belgium, you can move Gascony to Burgundy to block England, and your fleets can still move to MAO to prepare to attack them next turn.       :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country

                  :op1 (h / have-03
                        :ARG0 (c2 / country
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "England"))
                        :ARG1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Holland")))
                  :op2 (m / move-01

                              :mod c2
                              :location (p3 / province
                                    :name (n4 / name
                                          :op1 "Burgundy")))
                        :ARG2 p3)
                  :op3 (d / defend-01
                        :ARG0 c2
                        :ARG1 (p4 / province
                              :name (n5 / name
